    var dataLayer = window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];

    GaUtils = {};
    /**
     * @param productObj Object {"name": "%s", "id": "%s", "price": "%s", "brand": "%s", "category": "%s", "variant": "%s", "quantity": "%s"}
     */
    GaUtils.gaRemoveFromCart = function(productObj) {
        window.dataLayer.push({
            "event": "addToCart",
            "ecommerce": {
                "remove": {
                    'products': [productObj]
                }
            }
        });
    };

    /**
     * @param productObj Object {"name": "%s", "id": "%s", "price": "%s", "brand": "%s", "category": "%s", "variant": "%s", "quantity": "%s"}
     */
    GaUtils.gaAddToCart = function(productObj) {
        window.dataLayer.push({
            "event": "addToCart",
            "ecommerce": {
                "add": {
                    "products": [productObj]
                }
            }
        });

        window.dataLayer.push({
            'productAddToCart': productObj
        });
    };

    /**
     * @param productObj Object {"name": "%s", "id": "%s", "price": "%s", "brand": "%s", "category": "%s", "variant": "%s", "quantity": "%s"}
     */
    GaUtils.gaProductClick = function (productObj)
    {
        var list = "";
        if (typeof(productObj.list) !== "undefined") {
            list = productObj.list;
            delete productObj.list;
        }
        window.dataLayer.push({
            "event": "productClick",
            "ecommerce": {
                "click": {
                    "actionField": {"list": list},
                    "products": [productObj]
                }
            }
        });
    };

    /**
     * @param productObj Object {"name": "%s", "id": "%s", "price": "%s", "brand": "%s", "category": "%s", "variant": "%s", "quantity": "%s"}
     */
    GaUtils.gaProductImpression = function(productObj)
    {
        window.dataLayer.push({
            'ecommerce': {
                "currencyCode": "RON",
                "impressions": [productObj]
            }
        });
    };

    GaUtils.gaProductImpressions = function(productObjList)
    {
        window.dataLayer.push({
            "currencyCode": "RON",
            "impressions": productObjList
        });
    };

    /**
     * Data layer Product View Details
     * @param productObj
     */
    GaUtils.gaProductDetails = function(productObjList)
    {
        window.dataLayer.push({
            'ecommerce': {
                'detail': {
                    'actionField': {'list': productObjList[0].category},    // 'detail' actions have an optional list property.
                    'products': productObjList
                }
            }
        });
        window.dataLayer.push({
            'productDetails' : {
                'ecommerce': {
                    'detail': {
                        'actionField': {'list': productObjList[0].category},
                        'products': productObjList
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    };


    /**
     * @param products = array of productObj Object {"name": "%s", "id": "%s", "price": "%s", "brand": "%s", "category": "%s", "variant": "%s", "quantity": "%s"}
     */
    GaUtils.gaGoToCheckout = function(products) {
        if (!products.length) {
            return;
        }
        window.dataLayer.push({
            "event": "checkout",
            "ecommerce": {
                "checkout": {
                    "actionField": {"step": 1},
                    "products": products
                }
            }
        });
    };

    /**
     * @param orderData Object {"id": "%s", "affiliation": "%s", "revenue": "%s", "tax":"%s", "shipping": "%s", "coupon": "%s"}
     * @param products
     */
    GaUtils.gaFinishOrder = function(orderData, products)
    {
        window.dataLayer.push({
            "ecommerce": {
                "purchase": {
                    "actionField": orderData,
                    "products": products
                }
            }
        });
    };

    /**
     * @param transaction Object
     * @param cart Object
     * @param products
     */
    GaUtils.gaTransactionSuccess = function(transaction, cart, products)
    {
        window.dataLayer.push({
            "event": "transaction",
            "transaction": {
                "id": transaction.id,
                "affiliation": transaction.affiliation,
                "revenue": transaction.revenue,
                "tax": transaction.tax,
                "shipping": transaction.shipping,
                "coupon": transaction.coupon,
                "payment": transaction.payment,
                "delivery": transaction.delivery,
                "type": transaction.type
            },
            "cart":({
                "cartTotal": cart.cartTotal,
                "cartValue": cart.cartValue,
                "products": products
            })
        });
    };

    /**
     * Send promo details
     * @param promoObj Object {"id": "%s", "name": "%s", "creative": "%s", "position":"%s", "destinationUrl": "%s"}
     */
    GaUtils.gaGoToPromo = function(promoObj) {
        window.dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'promotionClick',
            'ecommerce': {
                'promoClick': {
                    'promotions': [
                        {
                            'id': promoObj.id,
                            'name': promoObj.name,
                            'creative': promoObj.creative,
                            'position': promoObj.position
                        }]
                }
            },
            'eventCallback': function() {
                document.location = promoObj.destinationUrl;
            }
        });
    };

    GaUtils.gaCriteoHome = function(criteo) {
        window.dataLayer.push({
            "event": "crto_homepage",
            "crto": {
                "email": criteo.email
            }
        });
    }

    GaUtils.gaCriteoListing = function(criteo) {
        window.dataLayer.push({
            "event": "crto_listingpage",
            "crto": {
                "email": criteo.email,
                "products": criteo.products
            }
        });
    }

    /*--== DELETE COOKIES --==*/
    function readCookie(name) {
        var nameEQ = name + "=";
        var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
        for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
            while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
            if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
        }
        return null;
    }

    (function() {
        var value = readCookie('gdpr_w');

        if(value == 'false') {

            document.cookie = "wipa_s=false; expires=Thu, 18 Dec 2013 12:00:00 UTC; path=/";
            document.cookie = "wipa_v=false; expires=Thu, 18 Dec 2013 12:00:00 UTC; path=/";
            document.cookie = "wipak=false; expires=Thu, 18 Dec 2013 12:00:00 UTC; path=/";
            document.cookie = "__utma=false; expires=Thu, 18 Dec 2013 12:00:00 UTC; path=/";

        }else{

            var wpa = document.createElement('script');
            wpa.type = 'text/javascript';
            wpa.async = 0;
            wpa.src = '//pa.7w.ro/js/trk_v3_.js?r=' + Math.random().toString().substring(2);
            var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
            s.parentNode.insertBefore(wpa, s);
        }
    })();

    <script>
        jQuery(document).ready(function () {
            var $ = jQuery;

            $.ajax({
                url: '/checkout/onepage/refreshFormKey?time=' + Date.now(),
                method: 'post',
                data: {time: Date.now()},
                timeout: 3000,
                cache: false,
                dataType: 'json',
                async: true,
                success: function (response) {
                    $('.login-form input[name="form_key"]').val(response.form_key);
                    $('.login-form input[type="submit"]').attr("disabled", false);

                    window.flanco_form_key = response.form_key;
                    window.is_form_key_updated = true;
                }
            })
        })
    </script>

            'maxPrice': ''
        },

        'productsSkus': productsSkus,
        'searchRtbSkus': '137648,146054,144107,137649,141129',

    });

    function pclick($thisElem, productObj) {
        window.dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'productClick',
            'ecommerce': {
                'click': {
                    'actionField': {'list': productObj.list},      // Optional list property.
                    'products': [{
                        'name': productObj.name,                      // Name or ID is required.
                        'id': productObj.id,
                        'price': productObj.price,
                        'brand': productObj.brand,
                        'category': productObj.category,
                        'position': productObj.position
                    }]
                }
            },
            'eventCallback': function () {
                document.location = $thisElem.attr('href');
            }
        });
    }

        "email": "",
        "products": ["137648","146054","144107","137649","141129","145932","85774","141179","141958","112071","111989","118696","141180","142860","146451","141387","146810","117862","126425","129078","144967","145579","146077","145986","145987","147005","96660","139329","139330","146964","147003","147004","147008","139331","141895","145577","146078","89964","147006","137713"]

        if(jQuery(this).data('fb')){
            fbq('track', 'AddToCart', {
                content_name: jQuery(this).data('fb').name,
